<s> Make sure that the upper left corner of the square is adjacent to the fourth row of the vertical line </s>===<s> square ( b ) ^ column ( a ) ^ block ( c ) ^ location ( w1 ) ^ block-location ( c , w1 ) ^ upper_left ( b , c ) ^ block ( d ) ^ location ( w2 ) ^ block-location ( d , w2 ) ^ right_side ( a , d , 3 ) ^ spatial-rel ( east , 0 , w2 , w1 ) </s>
<s> Finally , create a column of size 5 to the left of the square </s>===<s> column ( e ) ^ height ( e , 5 ) ^ column ( a ) ^ left ( e , a ) </s>
<s> Make sure that the top end of the column is next to the second row of the vertical line </s>===<s> column ( e ) ^ column ( a ) ^ block ( f ) ^ location ( w3 ) ^ block-location ( f , w3 ) ^ upper_right ( e , f ) ^ block ( g ) ^ location ( w4 ) ^ block-location ( g , w4 ) ^ left_side ( a , g , 1 ) ^ spatial-rel ( west , 0 , w4 , w3 ) </s>
